# Text Elements
Priority Queue ^Obkwma4m

        int prio = o.getPriority();
        if (queue.isEmpty()){
            queue.add(o); 
            return;
        }
        ListIterator<Priority> iter = queue.listIterator();
        int index = 0;
        while (iter.hasNext()) {
            Priority p = iter.next();
            if (prio < p.getPriority()) {

                queue.add(index, o);
                break; 
            }
            index++;
        } ^9nOBxGrg
